* Word Tree / Roget's Thesaurus


﻿* Class I. Words Expressing Abstract Relations

** Section I. Existence

*** 1. Being, in The Abstract

***** existence 1

 + entity           n.实体，统一体         [en-ti-ty]
 + extant           a.现存的，传世的        [ex-tant]
 + substantive      a.根本的；独立存在的      [sub-stan-tive]

***** inexistence 2

 + nil              n.无，零            [nil]
 + obliterate       v.涂掉，擦掉          [o-blit-e-rate]

*** 2. Being, In The Concrete

***** 3. substantiality

***** unsubstantiality 4

 + ethereal         a.太空；轻巧的         [e-the-re-al]
 + incogitant       a.无思想的，考虑不周的     [in-cog-i-tant]
 + vacuous          a.发呆的，愚笨的        [vac-u-ous]

*** 3. Formal Existence

***** intrinsicality 5

 + ethos            n.(个人、团体或民族)道德风貌，思潮，信仰 [e-thos]
 + hereditary       a.祖传的，世袭的        [he-red-i-tar-y]
 + immanent         a.内在的；普遍存在的      [im-ma-nent]
 + inborn           a.天生的，天赋的        [in-born]
 + indigenous       a.土产的，本地的        [in-dig-e-nous]
 + innate           a.生来的，天赋的        [in-nate]
 + virtual          a.实质上的，实际上的      [vir-tu-al]

***** 6. extrinsicality

*** 4. Modal Existence

***** state 7

 + category         n.类别，范畴          [cat-e-go-ry]
 + fungi            n.菌类，蘑菇          [fun-gi]

 + adventitious     a.偶然的            [ad-ven-ti-tious]

 + predicament      n.困境，窘境          [pre-dic-a-ment]

 + consistency      n.一致性；坚实度，可靠性；不矛盾 [con-sist-en-cy]
 + consistent       a.前后一致的          [con-sist-ent]
 + consonant        a.调和的，一致的        [con-so-nant]
 + correspondent    a.符合的；n.记者       [cor-re-spond-ent]
 + germane          a.有密切关系的；贴切的     [ger-mane]
 + harmony          n.相符，一致；协调，匀称    [har-mo-ny]
 + parallelism      n.平行，类似          [par-al-lel-ism]
 + pertinent        a.有关的，相关的        [per-ti-nent]
 + rapport          n.和睦，意见一致        [rap-port]
 + regulate         v.管制；调整          [reg-u-late]

 + incongruity      n.不协调，不相称        [in-con-gru-i-ty]

* Division II. Intersocial Volition

** Section I. General Intersocial Volition
